  annotations:
    acme.cert-manager.io/http01-edit-in-place: "true"
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: mymicroservices-issuer
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/backend-protocol: HTTPS
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /$2
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/secure-backends: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/use-forwarded-headers: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/use-regex: "true"
  name: ingress
  namespace: mymicroservices

  ingressClassName: nginx
  rules:
  - host: mymicroservices.com
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: authentication-svc
            port:
              number: 5100
        path: /authentications(/|$)(.*)
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:

            name: cart-svc
            port:
              number: 5500
        path: /carts(/|$)(.*)
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: customer-svc
            port:
              number: 5300
        path: /customers(/|$)(.*)
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: order-svc
            port:
              number: 5600
        path: /orders(/|$)(.*)
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: product-svc
            port:
              number: 5400
        path: /products(/|$)(.*)
        pathType: Prefix

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to ${NAMESPACE}/Ingress/${INGRESS_API_NAME}:
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/configuration-snippet: |
      limit_req_status 429;
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-burst-multiplier: "76608000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-connections: "25536"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-rate: "1024"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-rate-after: "10240"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-rps: "3000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: 200m
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-connect-timeout: "6000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-read-timeout: "6000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-send-timeout: "6000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/rewrite-target: /$1
  name: ${INGRESS_API_NAME}
  namespace: ${NAMESPACE}
spec:
  ingressClassName: nginx
  rules:
  - host: ${INGRESS_API_HOST}
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: ${INGRESS_SVC_NAME}
            port:
              number: ${INGRESS_SVC_PORT}
        path: /(.*)
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - ${INGRESS_API_HOST}
    secretName: ${INGRESS_SECRET}

kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    traefik.ingress.kubernetes.io/router.middlewares: wordpress-https-redirect@kubernetescrd,
      wordpress-add-forwarded-proto@kubernetescrd
  name: traefik-ingress-wordpress
  namespace: wordpress
spec:
  ingressClassName: traefik
  rules:
  - host: pre-datacenter.ucol.mx
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: wordpress
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /wordpress
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: wordpress
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /simple-wordpress
        pathType: Prefix
      - backend:
          service:
            name: admin-wordpress
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /admin-wordpress
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - pre-datacenter.ucol.mx
    secretName: microbot-data

---

metadata:

    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/scheme: internet-facing
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/subnets:
    - YOUR SUBNET
    alb.ingress.kubernetes.io/target-type: ip
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: alb
  name: zeppelin-ingress
  namespace: zeppelin
spec:
  rules:
  - http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: zeppelin-server
            port:
              number: 80
        path: /
        pathType: Prefix

policy add-safe-to-evict applied to zitadel/Ingress/zitadel-ingress:
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  annotations:
    cert-manager.io/clusterissuer: letsencrypt-prod
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/backend-protocol: HTTP
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/force-ssl-redirect: "true"
  name: zitadel-ingress
  namespace: zitadel
spec:
  ingressClassName: nginx
  rules:
  - host: zitadel.calloc.tech
    http:
      paths:
      - backend:
          service:
            name: my-zitadel
            port:
              number: 8080
        path: /
        pathType: Prefix
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - zitadel.calloc.tech
    secretName: zitadel-server-tls

---
